# War for Balkans
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.2
	title = ww1_ottoman.2.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_defensive_war_with = SER
		has_defensive_war_with = GRE
		has_defensive_war_with = BUL
		date < 1914.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
		}	
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

###Civil war over, recovery idea
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.5
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_hareket_ordusu_uprising
			has_country_flag = TUR_nationalist_uprising
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
			days = 360
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_ottoman.6
			days = 360
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.6
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		remove_ideas = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.7
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		has_civil_war = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
	}
}

# Mehmed V death
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.8
	title = ww1_ottoman.8.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		date > 1918.7.2
		has_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
		OR = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_v
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_osman_iv
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulhamid_ii
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = interwar_mehmed_vi_succeeded_mehmed_v
			set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_v_dies
			retire_character = TUR_mehmed_v
			TUR_mehmed_vi = {
				set_character_name = "TUR_mehmed_vi"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = TUR_mehmed_v
					}
				}
				promote_character = TUR_mehmed_vi
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				}
				remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				add_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.8.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = TUR_mehmed_v
			TUR_mehmed_vi = {
				set_character_name = "TUR_mehmed_vi"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = TUR_mehmed_v
					}
				}
				promote_character = TUR_mehmed_vi
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				}
				remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				add_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
			}
		}
	}
}

###Mehmed V dies Yusuf succeeds
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.9
	title = ww1_ottoman.9.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.9.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1918.7.2
		OR = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_v
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		has_character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_osman_iv
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.9.a
		set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_v_dies
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		retire_character = TUR_mehmed_v
		TUR_yusuf_izzeddin = {
			set_character_name = "TUR_yusuf_i"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = TUR_mehmed_v
				}
			}
			promote_character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			add_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
	}
}

###Yusuf Izzettin dead
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.10
	title = ww1_ottoman.10.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.10.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1916.2.1
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = mustafa_enver_cemal
			has_country_flag = TUR_three_pasha_government
			has_government = fascism
			has_global_flag = sevket_alive
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
			}
			has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.10.a
		retire_character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
		set_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
		custom_effect_tooltip = vahdettin_succeeds_mehmed_tt
	}
}

#Cairo and Alexandria are seized- event by Undead Unicorn :)
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.15
	title = ww1_ottoman.15.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_turkish_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		446 = {
			owns_or_subject_of = no
			controls_or_subject_of = yes
		}
		447 = {
			owns_or_subject_of = no
			controls_or_subject_of = yes
		}
		has_war = yes
		has_capitulated = no
		has_global_flag = great_war
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.15.a
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = 125
		set_country_flag = ottomans_hold_cairo_and_alexandria
	}
}

#We take Egypt after op- also by UU ;)
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.16
	title = ww1_ottoman.16.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_turkish_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ottomans_hold_cairo_and_alexandria
			has_subject = EGY
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = EGY
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.16.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						has_country_flag = great_war_loser
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = EGY
						is_core_of = SUD
						is_core_of = DAR
					}
				}
				# Take Suez and Ottoman core states
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 447
							state = 453
							is_core_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ROOT
					else = {
						# The others belongs to the Khedivate
						transfer_state_to = EGY
					}
				}
				# Annex it if Egypt is no longer has any Egyptian core state
				EGY = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_owned_state = {
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							annex_country = {
								target = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# No longer puppet of the defeated one
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_subject = EGY
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				}
				end_puppet = EGY
			}
			EGY = {
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				# Pro Ottoman Khedive
				promote_character = EGY_abbas_ii_helmy
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				# Fix Senussian border
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = LBA
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 552
								state = 767
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = LBA
					}
				}
			}
			# Puppet Khedivate
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_subject = EGY }
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = EGY
					autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
					freedom_level = 0.8
				}
				# For the Ottoman socialist path
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					EGY = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = communism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
					}
					# For the other paths
					else = {
						EGY = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_popularities = {
								democratic = 34
								neutrality = 65
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Germany asked about Turkish Egypt- UU once more :DDDDDDDDDD
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.17
	title = ww1_ottoman.17.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_turkish_pact
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	#Blank Cheque
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		TUR = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_ottoman.18
				hours = 8
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				give_resource_rights = {
					receiver = GER
					state = 291
				}
				give_resource_rights = {
					receiver = GER
					state = 676
				}
				give_resource_rights = {
					receiver = GER
					state = 292
				}
				give_resource_rights = {
					receiver = GER
					state = 678
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Demand Egyptian Neutrality
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
		}
		give_guarantee = EGY
		TUR = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_ottoman.19
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

#Germany gives Blank Cheque- me again
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.18
	title = ww1_ottoman.18.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_turkish_pact
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	#ebic B)
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 95
		}
		add_state_claim = 447
		add_state_claim = 453
		create_wargoal = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = EGY
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 291
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 676
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 292
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 678
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_idea_german_blank_cheque
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ottoman_egypt_guaranteed
		}
	}
	#on second thoughts...
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.18.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_stability < 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_war_support < 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = EGY
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.21
	title = ww1_ottoman.21.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spr_civil_war_faction_defeated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = {
				set_country_flag = TUR_arab_independence
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ASR
				}
				ASR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HJZ
				}
				HJZ = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = YEM
				}
				YEM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.21.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Crisis: Hareket Ordusu (Third Army) against Islamists
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.22
	title = ww1_ottoman.22.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_in_istanbul
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.35
				states = {
					356
					340
					911
					339
					342
					164
					899
					790
					348
					354
					1034
					355
					353
					352
					758
					803
					106
					760
					761
					759
					788
					184
					731
					454
					756
					757
					858
					856
					852
				}
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
					}
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 18
					fascism = 64
					communism = 0
					neutrality = 18
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				keep_political_leader = yes
				PREV = {
					TUR_ismail_enver = {
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					promote_character = personalistic_dictatorship

		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_PROTECT_DEMOCRACY
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_PROTECT_DEMOCRACY
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.28.b
		trigger = {
			fascism < 0.25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_ottoman.119
				days = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_AI_HISTORICAL_THREE_PASHA_GOVERNMENT
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = HISTORICAL_TRIUMVIRATE
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = TUR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
					has_country_flag = TUR_AI_TUR_vatan_ve_hurriyet_cemiyeti_path
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_VATAN_VE_HURRIYET_CEMIYETI

# Arabian Revolt - Deal with Faisal
######################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.46
	title = ww1_ottoman.46.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.46.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_and_pashas
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = SYR
			NOT = {
				state = 680
				state = 829
				state = 857
				state = 859
				state = 884
			}
		}
		has_war_with = HJZ
		has_global_flag = great_arabian_revolt
		SYR = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.46.a		#Independence for Syria
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SYR
					is_claimed_by = SYR
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 680
					state = 829
					state = 857
					state = 859
					state = 884
				}
			}
			SYR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SYR
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HJZ
				}
				transfer_state_to = HJZ
			}
			SYR = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
				}
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 100
				}
			}
		}
		HJZ = {
			clear_all_relations = yes
			give_military_access = SYR
			give_guarantee = SYR
		}
		SYR = {
			give_military_access = HJZ
			give_guarantee = HJZ
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				surrender_progress < 0.05
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				HJZ = { has_capitulated = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.46.b		#Ignor Faisal
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TUR
				is_core_of = SYR
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						state = 829
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
					}
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = TUR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

# Purchase Two Battleships From Germany

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.92
	title = ww1_ottoman.92.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.92.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR		#will be decision
		GER = {
			exists = yes
		}
		date > 1910.9.12
		has_start_date < 1914.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = GER
			has_global_flag = TUR_GER_battleship_purchase
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.92.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opda_lira
			}
			TUR_add_debt_0492 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = opda_lira
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_german_ship_purchase
				days = 360
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = germany_transfers_ships

				transfer_ship = {
					prefer_name = "SMS Kurfürst Friedrich Wilhelm"
					type = battleship
					target = TUR
				}
				transfer_ship = {
					prefer_name = "SMS Weissenburg"
					type = battleship
					target = TUR
				}
			}

				limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
					create_ship = {
					type = ship_hull_light_1
					equipment_variant = "S138 Class"
					creator = GER
					name = "Gayret-i Vataniyye"
				}

					type = ship_hull_light_1
					equipment_variant = "S138 Class"

		# owns_state = 678

	}

		}

					state = 292
					state = 678
					state = 905
					state = 918
				}
			}
			add_core_of = JBS
			transfer_state_to = JBS
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.99.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			end_puppet = JBS
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = JBS }
				JBS = { leave_faction = yes }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = JBS

				}
				white_peace = JBS
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JBS
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

			}

							y = 0
						}

							x = 0
							y = 1
						}

							y = 2
						}

							y = 0

					}

country_event = {
	id = ottoman.3
	title = ottoman.3.t
	desc = ottoman.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.3.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_halim
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = theocracy_ideology
				 	traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = ottoman.9 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				is_puppet_of = TUR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_subject_of = TUR
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_government = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				TUR = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.8.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = { 
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = ottoman.10 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_guaranteed = PREV
					NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_subject = PREV
					NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#coup after savior officers
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.36
	title = ottoman.36.t
	desc = ottoman.36.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.36.a
		clr_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_halim
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = theocracy_ideology
					traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#government struggle intervene
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.37
	title = ottoman.37.t
	desc = ottoman.37.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.37.a
		clr_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_halim
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = theocracy_ideology
					traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = TUR_CUP_prepares_coup_mission
			}
			remove_mission = TUR_CUP_prepares_coup_mission
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = TUR_CUP_coup_averted
			}
			remove_mission = TUR_CUP_coup_averted
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
  				uncomplete_children = yes
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
  				uncomplete_children = yes
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#intervene in elections
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.38
	title = ottoman.38.t
	desc = ottoman.38.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.38.a
		clr_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_halim
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = theocracy_ideology
					traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = TUR_CUP_prepares_coup_mission
			}
			remove_mission = TUR_CUP_prepares_coup_mission
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = TUR_CUP_coup_averted
			}
			remove_mission = TUR_CUP_coup_averted
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
  				uncomplete_children = yes
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
  				uncomplete_children = yes
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = {
		text = ottoman.42.t1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_elections_of_1912
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = ottoman.42.t2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_elections_of_1912
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_reaffirm_loyalty_of_the_army
				}
				complete_national_focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_elections_of_1912
		}
	}
	desc = ottoman.42.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1912.1.1
		date < 1913.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
			has_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
		}
		has_elections = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.42.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		add_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reaffirm_loyalty_of_the_army
			}
			complete_national_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
		}
		set_country_flag = ittihadist_victory
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = TUR_savior_officer_coup_mission
		}
	}
}

###Elections late 1912
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.45
	title = ottoman.45.t
	desc = ottoman.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1912.6.1
		date < 1913.1.1
		has_country_leader = {
			character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		has_elections = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
			name = TUR_neutrality_party
		}
	}
	option = {
		###Ittihad victory
		name = ottoman.45.a
		set_country_flag = ittihadist_victory
		TUR_mahmud_sevket = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 100
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			set_politics = {
			    ruling_party = neutrality
    		    election_frequency = 48
			    elections_allowed = yes
		    }
			add_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reaffirm_loyalty_of_the_army
			}
			complete_national_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_PROTECT_DEMOCRACY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_VATAN_VE_HURRIYET_CEMIYETI
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = HISTORICAL_TRIUMVIRATE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_FORM_A_LEFTIST_PARLIAMENT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		###Liberal victory
		name = ottoman.45.b
		set_country_flag = liberal_victory
		promote_character = TUR_mehmed_kamil
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.3
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_plot
			TUR_decrease_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty = yes
		}
		TUR_remove_minority_focuses = yes
		set_country_flag = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reaffirm_loyalty_of_the_army
			}
			complete_national_focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TUR_ai_behavior
					option = TUR_HURRIYET_VE_ITILAF
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ottoman.473
	title = ottoman.473.t
	desc = ottoman.473.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.473.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = TUR
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_diplomatic_isolation_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_democratic_party_value
				value = party_popularity@democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
				value = party_popularity@neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_communism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@communism
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_fascism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_elections = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TUR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				end_wars = yes
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = ottoman_democratic_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = ottoman_communism_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = ottoman_fascism_party_value
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.474 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.473.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.475 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

			has_war_with = GER

		months = 1
	}

			}

			}
		}

				add = 50

					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				is_puppet_of = TUR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_subject_of = TUR

				add = 25
				has_government = FROM

			modifier = {

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25

					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				TUR = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {

				}

					is_major = yes

				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes

				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #islamist victory in elections
	id = ottoman.118
	title = ottoman.118.t
	desc = ottoman.118.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_conservative_victory
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = TUR_pardon_conservatives
		is_power_balance_in_range = {
			id = TUR_conservative_liberal
			range < TUR_conservative_liberal_conservative_balanced
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_conservatives_in_charge
			has_country_flag = TUR_al_qahtaniya_empowered
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.118.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_unlock_said_i_nursi_path
		set_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_path
		set_country_flag = TUR_conservatives_in_charge
		clr_country_flag = TUR_liberals_in_charge
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = TUR_islamist_party_long
			name = TUR_islamist_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_leader
					has_country_flag = TUR_mustafa_sabri_leader
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_i_nursi
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conservatism
					traits = { islamist_modern_leader grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_leader
			}
			promote_character = TUR_said_i_nursi
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_mustafa_sabri_leader
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mustafa_sabri
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_modern_islamism_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_synthesis_of_the_old_and_the_new
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_increase_medrese_education_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_increase_medrese_education_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_form_volunteers_from_conservatives_done
				has_war = no
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_conservative_volunteers1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_form_volunteers_from_conservatives_done
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_conservative_volunteers2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_increase_sect_membership_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_empowered_sects
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_reform_mecelle_done
			}
			add_ideas = reformed_mecelle2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_guarantee_personal_freedoms_done
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_guaranteed_human_right
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = reformed_mecelle_done
			}
			remove_ideas = reformed_mecelle
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = secular_civil_code_done
			}
			remove_ideas = secular_civil_code
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = autonomous_civil_code_done
			}
			remove_ideas = autonomous_civil_code
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_status_of_autonomy_done
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_autonomous_vilayets
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		country_event = ottoman.164
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #population exchange between the ottomans
	id = ottoman.124
	title = ottoman.124.t
	desc = ottoman.124.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.124.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_state = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece1
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece1 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_1
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_core_of_turkey_for_tt }
							add_core_of = TUR
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_greek_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = GRE
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_pontus_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = PON
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece2 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_state = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece3
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece3 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_3
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_core_of_turkey_for_tt }
							add_core_of = TUR
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_greek_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = GRE
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_pontus_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = PON
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece4 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_state = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece5
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece5 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_5
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_core_of_turkey_for_tt }
							add_core_of = TUR
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_greek_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = GRE
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_no_longer_pontus_core_tt }
							remove_core_of = PON
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece6 }
						add_manpower = var:TUR.TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_state_population_6
					}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_send_greeks_to_greece
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GRE
					modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = { country_event = { id = ottoman.125 hours = 8 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 70
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.124.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = TUR_refused_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = { country_event = { id = ottoman.126 hours = 8 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}

	desc = ottoman.126.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ottoman.126.a

			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece2
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_deport_greeks
			set_country_flag = TUR_deport_greeks_flag
		}
		else = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = TUR_refused_to_population_exchange
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_not
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece
  				uncomplete_children = no
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

					target = MNT
					modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange

country_event = { #kurdish revolt 1
	id = ottoman.157
	title = ottoman.157.t
	desc = ottoman.157.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = TUR_forceful_assimilation_of_the_kurds
			progress > 0.07
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_kurdish_guerillas
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = TUR_kurd_state
					OR = {
						state = 350
						state = 829
						state = 881
						state = 884
					}
				}
				set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.1 }
				add_to_variable = {
					TUR_ottoman_resistance_growth = 0.15
				}
				remove_core_of = TUR
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
					}
					start_resistance = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.157.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = TUR_kurd_state
					OR = {

						state = 884
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_kurdish_minority_modify_resistance_target_negative_10_resistance_growth_negative_15
				remove_core_of = TUR
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
					}
					start_resistance = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5

						state = 352

						NOT = { state = 828 }

					add_core_of = ARM
				}
				add_claim_by = TUR
				if = {
					limit = {

					}

						state = 353
						state = 352
						state = 828
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_armenian_minority_modify_attrition_10_resistance_target_negative_35_resistance_growth_negative_15

country_event = { #asir rebellion
	id = ottoman.163
	title = ottoman.163.t
	desc = ottoman.163.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = ASR
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
		}
		date > 1910.10.1
		has_start_date < 1914.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = asir_rebellion
			country_exists = ASR
			has_government = democratic
			has_completed_focus = TUR_modern_islamism
			has_completed_focus = TUR_power_of_the_caliph
			has_completed_focus = TUR_for_the_good_of_the_arabs
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_asir_rebellion
	option = {
		name = ottoman.163.a
		set_global_flag = asir_rebellion
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 747
			}
			747 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_arab_minority_modify_resistance_target_10
				set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 747
				}
				owns_state = 662
			}
			662 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_arab_minority_modify_resistance_target_10
				set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.1 }
			}
		}
		activate_mission = TUR_brewing_asir_rebellion
		unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_truce_with_asir
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #death of Mehmed said
	id = ottoman.178
	title = ottoman.178.t
	desc = ottoman.178.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		OR = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_said
			}
			has_idea = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		date > 1914.1.10
		has_start_date < 1914.6.14
	}
	option = {
		set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_said_dead
		name = ottoman.178.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR_said_halim_advisor_role = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = TUR_mehmed_said
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = TUR_said_halim
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = theocracy_ideology
					traits = { TUR_conservative_politician2 grand_vizier }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_mehmed_said
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_mehmed_said
			add_ideas = TUR_said_halim
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_power_balance = {
					id = TUR_parliament_sultan
				}

	picture = GFX_report_event_picture_ottoman_balkan_war
	option = {
		name = ottoman.212.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { TUR_harbiyeli_officer_loyalty > 1 }
			}
			TUR_make_harbiyeli_officer_disloyalty = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
					has_completed_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_idea_chaos_balkans
				days = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_military_purges
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_idea_chaos_balkans
				days = 30
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SER
			modifier = large_decrease
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GRE
			modifier = small_decrease
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = MNT
			modifier = small_decrease
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BUL
			modifier = large_decrease
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar }
				}
				country_event = { id = ww1_ottoman.117 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Treaty of Batum
##############################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.112
	title = ww1_ottoman.112.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.112.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_upheaval_celebration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		# has_global_flag = brest_litovsk
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GEO
			has_war_with = ARM
			has_war_with = AZR
		}
		has_global_flag = caucasus_collapsed
		NOT = { has_global_flag = treaty_of_batum }
	}
	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = treaty_of_batum
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					has_country_flag = post_transcaucasia
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = post_transcaucasia }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
						state = 748
						state = 855
						state = 787
						state = 806
						state = 816
						state = 939
					}
					NOT = { state = 230 }
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
			}
			ARM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				give_military_access = ROOT
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = post_transcaucasia
					}
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = { original_tag = ARM }
					OR = {
						state = 818
						state = 938
					}
				}
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			MOU = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = no
						is_subject = no
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						OR = {
							has_government = ROOT
							NOT = { has_government = communism }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { give_guarantee = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.112.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_ottoman.132
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

# Death of Mehmed VI
#####################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.116
	title = ww1_ottoman.116.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.116.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		date > 1926.5.16
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_osman_iv
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_vi
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 8
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = interwar_abdulmejid_ii_succeeded_mehmed_vi
			set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_vi_dies
			retire_character = TUR_mehmed_vi
			TUR_abdulmecid_ii = {
				set_character_name = "TUR_abdulmecid_ii"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = TUR_mehmed_vi
					}
				}
				promote_character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.116.a
	}
}

###Muhtar pasa resigns
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.117
	title = ww1_ottoman.117.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.117.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_elections = yes
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			country_event = ww1_ottoman.130
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.117.a
		TUR_ahmed_muhtar = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_intervene_in_the_elections
			}
			clr_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
				name = TUR_sultanate_party
				long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1914.1.10
				}
				promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
				TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_said_halim
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = theocracy_ideology
						traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
			 	every_character = {
					TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
				}
				remove_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_intervene_in_the_elections
				}
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_kamil
			activate_mission = TUR_CUP_prepares_coup_mission
			activate_mission = TUR_CUP_coup_averted
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_muhtar_deposed
			hidden_effect = {
				TUR_mahmud_sevket = {
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
				name = TUR_neutrality_party
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = muhtar_pasa_resigns
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

#Ottomans Surrender
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.161
	title = ww1_ottoman.161.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.161.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fao
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.161.a
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				# Army
				every_state = {
					PREV = {
						delete_unit = {
							state = PREV
							disband = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = PREV }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_owned_by = FROM }
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = army_should_be_restricted
				country_lock_all_division_template = yes
				add_ideas = idea_army_restrictions

				# Territorial
				## Britain
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = ENG }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
							region = 228
							is_coastal = yes
							NOT = {
								state = 455
								state = 553
								state = 852
								state = 859
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = ENG
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_subject = AZR
						}
						AZR = {
							get_current_government_type = yes
							set_country_flag = protectorate
						}
						ENG = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = AZR
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
							}
						}
						AZR = {
							drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
							restore_previous_government_type = yes
							add_ideas = ENG_british_military_occupation
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								country_exists = BAK
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									BAK = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
								}
								AZR = {
									annex_country = {
										target = BAK
										transfer_troops = yes
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								BAK = {
									declare_war_on = {
										target = AZR
										type = civil_war
									}
									add_civil_war_target = AZR
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				## France
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
						region = 228
						is_coastal = yes
						NOT = {
							state = 455
							state = 859
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = FRA
				}
				## Syria
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
						region = 228
						NOT = {
							state = 447
							state = 453
							state = 859
							state = 677
							state = 680
							state = 884
							state = 1023
							state = 1029
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = SYR
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = SYR
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						SYR = { give_military_access = PREV }
					}
				}
				## Iraq
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = ENG }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
							region = 28
							NOT = {
								state = 676
								state = 879
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = ENG
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
							region = 28
							NOT = {
								state = 676
								state = 879
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = IRQ
					}
				}
				## Western Armenia
				if = {
					limit = {
						230 = {
							owner = {
								has_war_with = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
							OR = {
								region = 134
								state = 352
								state = 353
								state = 354
								state = 1022
								state = 1034
							}
						}
						230 = {
							owner = {
								transfer_state = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				### KARS REPUBLIC
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = treaty_of_batum
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							region = 134
							OR = {
								is_core_of = TUR
								state = 748
								state = 787
								state = 806
								state = 816
								state = 855
							}
						}
						add_core_of = KRS
						transfer_state_to = KRS
					}
					give_guarantee = KRS
					give_market_access = KRS
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ENG
						}
						ENG = {
							give_guarantee = KRS
							KRS = {
								get_current_government_type = yes
								set_country_flag = protectorate
							}
							set_autonomy = {
								target = KRS
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
							}
							KRS = {
								restore_previous_government_type = yes
								add_ideas = ENG_british_military_occupation
							}
						}
					}
					KRS = {
						set_country_flag = great_war_loser
						set_country_flag = member_of_central_powers
						add_ideas = idea_armistice
						set_country_flag = army_should_be_restricted
						country_lock_all_division_template = yes
						add_ideas = idea_army_restrictions
						inherit_technology = PREV
						give_military_access = PREV
						every_other_country = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_neighbor_of = PREV
									has_war_with = PREV.PREV
									is_in_faction_with = PREV.PREV
								}
							}
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 365
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit  = {
								is_neighbor_of = GEO
							}
							# Georgia supported them because they don't want Azerbaijan to expand west
							GEO = {

							limit = {

								is_core_of = ARM
							}
							transfer_state_to = ARM

					}
					if = {

							country_exists = AZR

							limit = {

								is_core_of = AZR
							}
							transfer_state_to = AZR
						}
					}
					if = {

							country_exists = GEO
						}
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								region = 134
								is_core_of = GEO
							}
							transfer_state_to = GEO
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {

							OR = {
								state = 417
								state = 877
							}
						}
						420 = {
							owner = {
								transfer_state = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				## The Straits
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = RUS
						NOT = { has_global_flag = russian_revolution }
					}
					every_state = {

							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes

					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ENG
					}
					every_state = {

							is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
							OR = {
								state = 347

								state = 861

							state = 679
							state = 878

				every_state = {

					}

				}

					limit = {

					HJZ = { load_oob = HJZ_1910 }
					ASR = { load_oob = ASR_1910 }
					YEM = { load_oob = YEM_1910 }
				}
				## The Gulf
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
						OR = {
							state = 804
							state = 904
							state = 905

							state = 658

							state = 886

					if = {

					}
					else = {
						PREV = {
							release = BHR
							release = QAT
							release = UAE
						}
					}
				}
				## The Balkans
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 898
						NOT = { country_exists = GRE } 
					}
					release = GRE
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_or_subject_FROM_trigger = yes
						OR = {
							state = 164
							state = 182
							state = 183
							state = 790

					}

					limit = {

						OR = {
							state = 184
							state = 185
							state = 200
							state = 345

					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 48
						NOT = { country_exists = BUL } 
					}
					release = BUL
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {

						OR = {
							state = 184

							state = 225

						NOT = { country_exists = SER } 
					}
					release = SER
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {

						OR = {
							state = 106
							state = 203

				leave_faction = yes
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {

					PREV = {
						remove_wargoal = {
							type = all
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					white_peace = PREV
					PREV = { give_military_access = PREV }
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					white_peace = PREV
					PREV = { give_military_access = PREV }
				}
				every_subject_country = {
					limit = {
						has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_emirate
					}
					clear_all_relations = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = great_war_loser
				set_country_flag = member_of_central_powers
				add_ideas = idea_armistice

				#entente divisions to cosntantinople
				every_other_country = {

					every_state = {

			}

			base = 100
		}

# Armistice of Mudros
news_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.162
	title = ww1_ottoman.162.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.162.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_civil_war_turkey
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	major = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.162.a
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.162.b
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = TUR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.162.c
		trigger = {
			has_war_together_with = TUR
			NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.162.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = TUR
				has_war_together_with = TUR
				original_tag = TUR
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_ottoman.163.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_turkish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.163.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			white_peace = FRA
			add_ideas = idea_armistice
			add_ideas = idea_army_restrictions
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = ENG

			ENG = {

				}

		else = {

					hours = 3
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				id = ww1_ottoman.162
				hours = 10
			}
		}
	}
